 Under Article 370 and 35A, Jammu and Kashmir had more privileges than other states of the country
 sansad se paarit sirf raksha, videsh or sanchaar maamalon ko chhodkar anya koi kanoon sidhe nahin lagu hote the

 Article 35-A laid down the rules of permanent citizenship and rights of citizens for the state of Jammu and Kashmir
 iske tahat jammu kashmir sarkaar un logon ko sthai nivasee maanati he jo 14 may 1954 ke pehle kashmir main bas gaye the

 isi tarah mahilaon ke maamle main bhi anuchhed 35 e bhedbhaav ko janm detaa he

 magar yadi kashmir kaa koi purush baahar kii ladki se shaadi karata he to us par yah niyam nahin lagu hote
